  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_55445019-fa65-4871-9666-09361b4680d1'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

    It felt like my soul was stolen from my body and shredded into useless, drown fabric. I was expecting this one to be the last book. I normally wouldn'<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    It felt like my soul was stolen from my body and shredded into useless, drown fabric. I was expecting this one to be the last book. I normally wouldn't mind but the book won't come out till JUNE so...<br /><br />But other than that I really loved it, I did not expect the time travel or the ending, and the relationship that's between Teague and Mina. Gosh I hate Brody<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>

  <span id="freeText12653743566360872363" style="display:none">I love this series but there are some things I didn't like about this book. First off I just want to mention that there still needs to be a lot of editing done to this book. Also the language is awkward at times and I can't imagine anyone speaking like that. <br /><br />Second, I felt like nothing happened or was accomplished in this book really. She just realized how the curse came to be which is good and all but doesn't really help move along the story too much. Everything just fell apart more in Mina's world but she really did nothing. I didn't like that. <br /><br />I do love the storyline for this series though. It's really unique and I love the Grimm fairy tales. The characters are fun and there is enough action in the book to be entertaining. I did enjoy the book even with its faults. I'll still read the next book which is the last one because I really want to find out how it ends.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1109978367?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hannah Stevenson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hannah Stevenson" href="/user/show/24366030-hannah-stevenson">Hannah Stevenson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1109978367" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11636344491169514692">This is the BEST book yet in the series! When I finished this book I would have squealed with giddiness at how excited I was about it but it was at 2 a.m. in the morning and my light-sleeper of a husband would not have appreciated that. Needless to say, I fell asleep with a smug smile on my face.<br/>So, my prediction did not come true in this book (I was thinking that there would be a Beauty in the Beast plot between Mina and Jared) but there is still a possibility of this happening in the next book</span>
  <span id="freeText11636344491169514692" style="display:none">This is the BEST book yet in the series! When I finished this book I would have squealed with giddiness at how excited I was about it but it was at 2 a.m. in the morning and my light-sleeper of a husband would not have appreciated that. Needless to say, I fell asleep with a smug smile on my face.<br />So, my prediction did not come true in this book (I was thinking that there would be a Beauty in the Beast plot between Mina and Jared) but there is still a possibility of this happening in the next book because there is going to be another one! YAY! I thought this would be the last. <br />This book was a little heavy on the love triangle, as all of the other books in these series were but I actually didn't mind it like I do in other books, maybe because there are other things to love about this book besides the love triangle thing perhaps (ahem, Twilight). And mostly because it is not too sappy and has a good pace and is not insta-ish (ahem, Twilight). There are plenty of foreshadowing who Mina will end up with but like I said there are other things to keep me interested about this book, although, I have to admit I want to know how the romance will all unfold with the next book (ahem, not like Twilight). <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11636344491169514692" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1059901591" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1059901591" />
    <a title="Elizabeth (Elzburg)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26150006-elizabeth-elzburg"><img alt="Elizabeth (Elzburg)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1542862303p2/26150006.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1059901591?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth (Elzburg)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth (Elzburg)" href="/user/show/26150006-elizabeth-elzburg">Elizabeth (Elzburg)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26150006-elizabeth-elzburg?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26150006-elizabeth-elzburg?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1059901591" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2703597720898761052">This review looks really big but it’s mostly small paragraphs and quotes so don’t be scared! <s>LOVEME</s><br/><br/>It felt weird and exciting to be finally reading a new book in this series. As you (of course) know, I read the first three books in the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13402447.UnEnchanted__An_Unfortunate_Fairy_Tale___1_' title='UnEnchanted (An Unfortunate Fairy Tale, #1) by Chanda Hahn' rel='nofollow noopener'>Unenchanted</a>/Unfortunate Fairy Tale series a few years back, and now I’ve been re-reading the series to finish it up. This fourth book was all new territory. <br/><br/>It started out kindaaaa… Slowww…ish? It was like the last book in that it was basically a contemporary nove</span>
  <span id="freeText2703597720898761052" style="display:none">This review looks really big but it’s mostly small paragraphs and quotes so don’t be scared! <s>LOVEME</s><br><br>It felt weird and exciting to be finally reading a new book in this series. As you (of course) know, I read the first three books in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13402447.UnEnchanted__An_Unfortunate_Fairy_Tale___1_" title="UnEnchanted (An Unfortunate Fairy Tale, #1) by Chanda Hahn" rel="nofollow noopener">Unenchanted</a>/Unfortunate Fairy Tale series a few years back, and now I’ve been re-reading the series to finish it up. This fourth book was all new territory. <br><br>It started out kindaaaa… Slowww…ish? It was like the last book in that it was basically a contemporary novel with what was going on. Brody’s noggin has been messed with so many times that he’s crazy enough to think he actually <i>likes</i> Mina, and he invites her to a ball. And we all know the thing about <b>balls</b>…<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Balls were full of fairy tale possibility.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Heheheheh. <s>Nice.</s><br><br>So the beginning of the book is just kinda about that and what ensues. A cool thing was that I actually learned something at this part. I present: <b>Chanda Hahn’s Guild to the Waltz:</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>“ Right foot forward, to the side, and feet together.” Her partner continued to give her tips. “Now left foot back, move to the side, feet together. Imagine an invisible box and your feet can only move along the outline of this box. Do you see it? Now listen to the orchestra. Do you hear it? Can you feel it?”</i>
</blockquote> I feel like this is some good information to know.<br><br>Since Nix and Brody are both on the water polo team they’re buddies, and I liked this dynamic. It made it so whenever Brody was around, Nix was too. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Nix flung his arm out toward the classroom they’d just left and almost clotheslined a poor unsuspecting student.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I love Nix. He’s kind of the opposite of Jared. He’s really nice. SPEAKING OF—<br><br>WHERE THE HELL WAS MY JARED!??!?! The reason I stopped reading this series all those years ago was because I didn’t want to read this if there wasn’t going to be any Jared in it. Well, uh, I was right in my assumption. There <i>are</i> definitely mentions of him, but he’s never actually in it. Just… Teague.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>It wasn’t fear that caused the single tear to cascade down her cheek, but sadness—at the loss of Jared. Looking into Jared’s face and seeing someone else’s hate-filled gaze was almost her undoing.</i>
</blockquote> I feel you, sister.<br><br>Teague was a butt. I mean, he’s always been an asshole, but in this book he goes next level asshole. He was never really that bad in past books, just an inconvenience really. In this book he’s really evil. He actually physically attacks and harms Mina, and for once you really believe him when he threatens her loved ones.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>This wasn’t a case of Jekyll and Hyde. This was Hyde on steroids.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>But Teague wasn’t the only bad-bitch fairy in town. Nah blood, that title belongs to Ever. I feel like it was kind of irrational how much I hated her my first time through this series. The reasons were because she was mean and because she was a love rival in regards to Jared. I was basically Juvia from Fairy Tail.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442471491i/16240459.png" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> I love Ever now. She’s usually pretty cool and funny. She’s not even that mean anymore.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Mina looked to Ever, and the girl shrugged her shoulders before answering. “You kinda stink.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>There were a lot of points like this in the book that amused me. I’ve scattered a lot of the quotes that made me chuckle throughout this review. But you know what didn’t make me chuckle?!??! The fact that Mina is actually pretty smart. <br><br>It’s kinda weird, you know? Having a heroine that isn’t a complete dumb-ass. It was nice, and Mina would figure things out before I would which usually doesn’t happen. Usually the author fills the book up with a million clues so by the time the character figures it out the reader already knew for half the book. I feel like it kept things moving.<br><br>While Mina was busy getting shit done, I was busy making false accusations. There were a couple parts where it felt like Hahn was hinting at something that was going to happen and I was like “OMG NOOOO OMG THIS IS TOTALLY GOING TO HAPPEN I <u>KNOW</u> IT 100%” But then… it didn’t happen. And it was awesome. This is also something that I like a lot about Gravity Falls. The episode starts and you’re like, “Oh, it’s going to be THAT kind of episode…” BUT THEN IT’S NOT AND IT’S AWESOME. I ALREADY SAID THAT BUT IT’S OKAY. WE’RE ALL FRIENDS HERE. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I literally wrote in my notes that I knew 100% that Ever and Nix were going to get together because it really felt that that was what Hahn was hinting to. But nothing happened and I was like yaaayy. It could still happen in the next book but at this point I don’t ship it. Also, after Brody got bitten by the wolf I thought he was going to turn into a werewolf… REALLY DODGED A BULLET WITH THAT ONE!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Unlike the last book (which only got fantastical towards the end of the book), Reign got busy quick and a lot went down. So much was going down that I actually thought to myself, “Everything’s happening! Nothing’s going to be left for the last book!” We find out a lot of much needed backstory which was awesome, and it wasn’t like just info dumps either. It was really unique with what went down, and heart breaking.<br><br>Can’t wait to read the last book, but at the same time I don’t want the story to end. I love these characters and have loved them for a long time.<br><br>SPEEEEEEEEEEAKING OF LOOOOOVE.<br>Here’s this fun thing I found, I’ll play for shits and giggles. My answer is below.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442471491i/16240460._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kill:</b> Brody, I don’t even have to contemplate that one. Well, except for the guy in the picture is the actor who played John Smith in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7747374.I_Am_Number_Four__Lorien_Legacies___1_" title="I Am Number Four (Lorien Legacies, #1) by Pittacus Lore" rel="nofollow noopener">I Am Number Four</a> movie, which did give me slight pause because Four is bae. Well, Nine and Adam are bae, but whatever.<br><b>Kiss:</b> Jared. Although I love him, he’s not really for mee. He’s for Mina. <br><b>Marry:</b> Nix!! That cutie patootie will be mine forevaarr!<br><br>Feel free to comment your answer below if you want! :)<br><br><br><i>Please give this review a "Like" if you've made it this far, and <a href="http://www.bit.ly/elzburg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">follow me</a> if you want more!</i><br><blockquote>
<i><b>Click these links to go read my other reviews for the Unenchanted Fairytale series!</b></i><br>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1362328233?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Unenchanted</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1380090777?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Fairest</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1059896464?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Fable</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1059901591?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Reign</a> &lt;--You are here.<br>Book 1.5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1394277187?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Jared’s Quest</a><br>Book 5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1396391517?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Forever</a>
</blockquote></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1130079739" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1130079739" />
    <a title="J. Kwong" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34069758-j-kwong"><img alt="J. Kwong" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408367411p2/34069758.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1130079739?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J. Kwong" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J. Kwong" href="/user/show/34069758-j-kwong">J. Kwong</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1130079739" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13271768855424638137">When I first started reading this series, I couldn't get over the awkwardness and choppiness of the writing style. However, I continued to read the series just because I love stories based on fairy tales and I have to say the premise of the series is quite unique and creative. I'm happy to say that the author has improved her writing style significantly and it really came through in the most recent book of this series (Reign). I was also worried that her creativity would wane by this 4th book bu</span>
  <span id="freeText13271768855424638137" style="display:none">When I first started reading this series, I couldn't get over the awkwardness and choppiness of the writing style. However, I continued to read the series just because I love stories based on fairy tales and I have to say the premise of the series is quite unique and creative. I'm happy to say that the author has improved her writing style significantly and it really came through in the most recent book of this series (Reign). I was also worried that her creativity would wane by this 4th book but I really enjoyed the story and thought that this was probably one of the best books in this series. I can't wait for the next book and highly recommend anyone following this series to read this 4th book.<br /><br />Writing style continues to need improvement but the author has truly come a long way. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13271768855424638137" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7148812081229088243">I preordered this book awhile back because my kids and I really enjoy Chanda Hahn's books. I was not disappointed. Since I started it I could not put it down. Now I know how it all started and all I can say is I was not expecting what I read. I loved it and I can't wait for book five, 2015 can't get here soon enough...lol. In this book we find out why the curse what really made Teague as bad as he is and we see more of Nix and Brody..but all I can think about is Jared. and if you've read the oth</span>
  <span id="freeText7148812081229088243" style="display:none">I preordered this book awhile back because my kids and I really enjoy Chanda Hahn's books. I was not disappointed. Since I started it I could not put it down. Now I know how it all started and all I can say is I was not expecting what I read. I loved it and I can't wait for book five, 2015 can't get here soon enough...lol. In this book we find out why the curse what really made Teague as bad as he is and we see more of Nix and Brody..but all I can think about is Jared. and if you've read the other books in this series than you'll love to hear about Ever before she turned to a Goth Pixie. I absolutely loved this book :)</span>

<div id="review_1097276107" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1097276107" />
    <a title="EmmiK" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34437178-emmik"><img alt="EmmiK" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434113717p2/34437178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1097276107?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2014</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1123542473" />
    <a title="Abby Shepard" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35074546-abby-shepard"><img alt="Abby Shepard" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411427753p2/35074546.jpg" /></a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer5123406353196849920">After making a decision that cost her one of the only people she cares about, Mina Grimm is left with nothing but a boatload of grief, lots of guilt, and an otherworldly prince who wants her dead. The fairytale curse that has been destroying her family for centuries has been the las thing in her mind, that is until the unthinkable happens. Mina's distant family members begin to fade from existence. It is clear that Mina will be next if she can't find a way to stop her relatives from disappearing</span>
  <span id="freeText5123406353196849920" style="display:none">After making a decision that cost her one of the only people she cares about, Mina Grimm is left with nothing but a boatload of grief, lots of guilt, and an otherworldly prince who wants her dead. The fairytale curse that has been destroying her family for centuries has been the las thing in her mind, that is until the unthinkable happens. Mina's distant family members begin to fade from existence. It is clear that Mina will be next if she can't find a way to stop her relatives from disappearing, and fast. But, when this task proves to involve her going back in time, and facing her most deadly enemy in his youth, will she be able to make it back alive? I recommend this book to anyone who likes the other books in this series, or who has read "The Grimm Legacy".</span>
  <a data-text-id="5123406353196849920" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6pz7/Abh7/wdnJBDSGzSwVzhlT9TsH39xUfC2N0DeTTBgn3hQscr1WX78FtwBTUV3AeGBXYewDTbl4xWvtlobw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jTKHXcwBCyG9p1wTIzI6myPUu5QHv2G4TaGzza4+JPCmLAFAiCfPCMXAPAsbW91PozKoriIR3HFTcf1DzeQ1qw==')})
  }
//]]>

  <span id="freeText16469307490822443074" style="display:none">Chanda Hahn is a New York Times and USA Today bestselling author of Reign An Unfortunate Fairy Tale. She was born in Seattle, WA, grew up in Nebraska and currently resides in Portland, Oregon with her husband and their twin children. She attended North Central University in Minneapolis Minnesota for Childrens Ministry.
